\index{mov.c@{mov.c}!add\_index\_entry@{add\_index\_entry}}
\index{add\_index\_entry@{add\_index\_entry}!mov.c@{mov.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{add\_index\_entry()}{add\_index\_entry()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int64\+\_\+t add\+\_\+index\+\_\+entry (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_stream}{A\+V\+Stream}} $\ast$}]{st,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{pos,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timestamp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{distance,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Add index entry with the given values, to the end of st-\/$>$internal-\/$>$index\+\_\+entries. Returns the new size st-\/$>$internal-\/$>$index\+\_\+entries if successful, else returns -\/1.

This function is similar to ff\+\_\+add\+\_\+index\+\_\+entry in libavformat/utils.\+c except that here we are always unconditionally adding an index entry to the end, instead of searching the entries list and skipping the add if there is an existing entry with the same timestamp. This is needed because the mov\+\_\+fix\+\_\+index calls this func with the same unincremented timestamp for successive discarded frames.

\index{mov.c@{mov.c}!find\_prev\_closest\_index@{find\_prev\_closest\_index}}
\index{find\_prev\_closest\_index@{find\_prev\_closest\_index}!mov.c@{mov.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find\_prev\_closest\_index()}{find\_prev\_closest\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} find\+\_\+prev\+\_\+closest\+\_\+index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_stream}{A\+V\+Stream}} $\ast$}]{st,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_index_entry}{A\+V\+Index\+Entry}} $\ast$}]{e\+\_\+old,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{nb\+\_\+old,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_o_v_stts}{M\+O\+V\+Stts}} $\ast$}]{ctts\+\_\+data,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{ctts\+\_\+count,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timestamp\+\_\+pts,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{flag,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{index,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{ctts\+\_\+index,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{ctts\+\_\+sample }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Find the closest previous frame to the timestamp\+\_\+pts, in e\+\_\+old index entries. Searching for just any frame / just key frames can be controlled by last argument \textquotesingle{}flag\textquotesingle{}. Note that if ctts\+\_\+data is not N\+U\+LL, we will always search for a key frame irrespective of the value of \textquotesingle{}flag\textquotesingle{}. If we don\textquotesingle{}t find any keyframe, we will return the first frame of the video.

Here the timestamp\+\_\+pts is considered to be a presentation timestamp and the timestamp of index entries are considered to be decoding timestamps.

Returns 0 if successful in finding a frame, else returns -\/1. Places the found index corresponding output arg.

If ctts\+\_\+old is not N\+U\+LL, then refines the searched entry by searching backwards from the found timestamp, to find the frame with correct P\+TS.

Places the found ctts\+\_\+index and ctts\+\_\+sample in corresponding output args.

\index{mov\_fix\_index@{mov\_fix\_index}!mov.c@{mov.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mov\_fix\_index()}{mov\_fix\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} mov\+\_\+fix\+\_\+index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_o_v_context}{M\+O\+V\+Context}} $\ast$}]{mov,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_stream}{A\+V\+Stream}} $\ast$}]{st }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Fix st-\/$>$internal-\/$>$index\+\_\+entries, so that it contains only the entries (and the entries which are needed to decode them) that fall in the edit list time ranges. Also fixes the timestamps of the index entries to match the timeline specified the edit lists.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mov\_read\_strf()}{mov\_read\_strf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} mov\+\_\+read\+\_\+strf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_o_v_context}{M\+O\+V\+Context}} $\ast$}]{c,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_i_o_context}{A\+V\+I\+O\+Context}} $\ast$}]{pb,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_o_v_atom}{M\+O\+V\+Atom}}}]{atom }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

An strf atom is a B\+I\+T\+M\+A\+P\+I\+N\+F\+O\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER struct. This struct is 40 bytes itself, but can have extradata appended at the end after the 40 bytes belonging to the struct.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} mov\+\_\+try\+\_\+read\+\_\+block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_i_o_context}{A\+V\+I\+O\+Context}} $\ast$}]{pb,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Tries to read the given number of bytes from the stream and puts it in a newly allocated buffer. This reads in small chunks to avoid allocating large memory if the file contains an invalid/malicious size value.
